    A seÂ­cond adÂ­justÂ­ment proÂ­blem faced by all gifÂ­ted perÂ­sons is due to their unÂ­comÂ­mon verÂ­saÂ­tiÂ­liÂ­ty. HolÂ­lingÂ­worth says:
